         <h6 class="record-heading">
          <a href="/2018/06/20/volvo-first-us-factory-south-carolina/" itemprop="url">
           <span itemprop="headline">
            Volvo opens doors to its first U.S. factory near Charleston, South Carolina
           </span>
          </a>
         </h6>
         <p class="subTitle hidden-tn" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
          150,000-unit facility will build new S60 sedan this year, half for export
         </p>
         <div class="description" itemprop="articleBody">
          <p>
           150,000-unit facility will build new S60 sedan this year, half for export.
          </p>

   <script>
    var waitForJquery = setInterval(bindToaster,100);
 
 	function bindToaster(){
 		if(typeof $ !== 'undefined'){
 			$(window).on('scroll', function() {
 				if ($(document).scrollTop() > 400) {
 					$('#toaster_autoblog-app').addClass('show').removeClass('hide');
 				} else {
 					$('#toaster_autoblog-app').removeClass('show').addClass('hide');
 				}
 			});
 
 			$('#toaster_autoblog-app .button-back').mouseout(function() {
 				setTimeout(function(){
 					$('#toaster_autoblog-app').removeClass('show').addClass('hide').attr('style','display:none !important' );
 
 					$.cookie('toaster_state', 'hidden',{expires:30, path:'/'});
 				}, 5000);
 			});
 
 			clearInterval(waitForJquery);
 		}
 	}
 
 	
 
 ;(window);

 AUTOBLOG.ads.adCall = function(ads, layout){
 	
 
     if (typeof(adSetInView) !== "function") { return; }
 
 	var devices = Boot.respond();
 
 	adSetHtNmAT('https://at.atwola.com');
 
 	if (typeof ads == 'string') { ads = AUTOBLOG.ads[ads]; } else if (ads == null) { ads = AUTOBLOG.ads.desktop; }
 
 	AUTOBLOG.ads.adCleanup();
 
 	for (var key in ads) {
 		var obj = ads['mn'] && ads || ads[key] || {};
 
 		if (obj.hasOwnProperty('mn')) {
 			if (document.getElementById(key)) {
 				adVis(key, 1);
 
                 if (obj['adType'] === 'text') { adsSetEAN(key, 'br'); }
 
                 htmlAdWH(obj['mn'],obj['width'],obj['height'],obj['adType'],key);
 
 				adVis(key, 0);
 
 				if (layout) { document.getElementById(key).setAttribute('data-adtype', layout); }
 
 				if (AUTOBLOG.settings.debug) {
 					var elem = document.getElementById(key),
                         val = key + ' ' + JSON.stringify(obj);
 
 					elem.setAttribute('data-toggle', 'popover');
 					elem.setAttribute('data-content', val);
 					elem.setAttribute('data-placement', 'bottom');
 				}
 			}
 		}
 	}
 
 	function adVis(key, value) {
 		if (value === 1) {
 			if (ads[key]['adSetInView']) { adSetInView( ads[key]['adSetInView'] ); }
 		} else if (value === 0) {
 			if (ads[key]['adSetInView']) { adSetInView('0'); }
 		}
 	}
 };
 
 AUTOBLOG.ads.adCleanup = function(){
 	var a = document.getElementById('ad-banner');
 
 	if (a != null && a.hasAttribute('style')) {
 		var els = [];
 
 		while (a) {
 			a.removeAttribute('style');
 			els.unshift(a);
 			a = a.parentNode;
 		}
 	}
 };

     htmlAdWH = function () {
         AUTOBLOG.main.log('htmlAdWH: not defined', arguments);
     };
 }

     AUTOBLOG.settings.adBlockEnabled = true;
